Here's a comprehensive breakdown:\\n\\n---\\n\\n## `ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable` — Definition and Usage\\n\\n### 1. Definition\\n\\n`ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable` is defined in [`raft/storage.go` (line 38)](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/storage.go?L36-38):\\n\\n```go\\n// ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable is returned by the Storage interface when the required\\n// snapshot is temporarily unavailable.\\nvar ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable = errors.New(\\\"snapshot is temporarily unavailable\\\")\\n```\\n\\nIt is specified as part of the `Storage` interface contract on the [`Snapshot()` method (lines 67–71)](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/storage.go?L67-71):\\n\\n```go\\n// Snapshot returns the most recent snapshot.\\n// If snapshot is temporarily unavailable, it should return ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable,\\n// so raft state machine could know that Storage needs some time to prepare\\n// snapshot and call Snapshot later.\\nSnapshot() (pb.Snapshot, error)\\n```\\n\\nThis is a **signal contract**: custom `Storage` implementations (e.g., those with async or disk-backed snapshot generation) return this to tell the Raft state machine \\\"not yet, try again later.\\\" The built-in [`MemoryStorage.Snapshot()`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/storage.go?L165-170) never returns this error — it's always immediately available.\\n\\n---\\n\\n### 2. How Snapshot Availability Is Checked During Log Catch-Up\\n\\nWhen a **lagging node rejoins** the cluster and needs to catch up, the leader handles it via [`maybeSendAppend()` in `raft/raft.go` (lines 447–506)](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/raft.go?L447-506). Here's the full flow:\\n\\n#### Step 1 — Try to send log entries\\nThe leader looks up the follower's [`Progress`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/tracker/progress.go?L30-80) tracker and tries to retrieve the entries from its next expected index (`pr.Next`):\\n\\n```go\\nterm, errt := r.raftLog.term(pr.Next - 1)\\nents, erre := r.raftLog.entries(pr.Next, r.maxMsgSize)\\n```\\n\\n#### Step 2 — Fall back to snapshot if entries are unavailable\\nIf `errt != nil || erre != nil` (i.e., the required entries have been compacted away — the node is too far behind), the leader falls back to sending a full snapshot:\\n\\n```go\\nif errt != nil || erre != nil { // send snapshot if we failed to get term or entries\\n    if !pr.RecentActive {\\n        // Ignore — follower hasn't been heard from recently\\n        return false\\n    }\\n\\n    m.Type = pb.MsgSnap\\n    snapshot, err := r.raftLog.snapshot()  // calls l.storage.Snapshot()\\n```\\n\\n#### Step 3 — Snapshot availability check\\n\\n[`raftLog.snapshot()`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/log.go?L170-175) first checks for an in-memory unstable snapshot, then delegates to the application's `Storage`:\\n\\n```go\\nfunc (l *raftLog) snapshot() (pb.Snapshot, error) {\\n    if l.unstable.snapshot != nil {\\n        return *l.unstable.snapshot, nil\\n    }\\n    return l.storage.Snapshot()\\n}\\n```\\n\\nBack in `maybeSendAppend()`, **this is where `ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable` is caught** [(lines 469–474)](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/raft.go?L469-474):\\n\\n```go\\nif err != nil {\\n    if err == ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable {\\n        r.logger.Debugf(\\\"%x failed to send snapshot to %x because snapshot is temporarily unavailable\\\", r.id, to)\\n        return false  // ← silently bail; will retry on next tick\\n    }\\n    panic(err) // any other error is fatal\\n}\\n```\\n\\n- **If `ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable`**: returns `false` — no message is sent this tick. The Raft heartbeat/tick cycle will cause `maybeSendAppend()` to be called again on the next tick, retrying the snapshot.\\n- **Any other error**: panics immediately (unrecoverable).\\n\\n#### Step 4 — Snapshot is sent and follower transitions to `StateSnapshot`\\n\\nIf the snapshot is available, the leader sends a `MsgSnap` message and transitions the follower's progress via [`pr.BecomeSnapshot(sindex)` (line 483)](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/raft.go?L483):\\n\\n```go\\nm.Snapshot = snapshot\\npr.BecomeSnapshot(sindex)  // sets pr.State = StateSnapshot, pr.PendingSnapshot = sindex\\n```\\n\\nWhile in [`StateSnapshot`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/tracker/state.go?L32-33), `IsPaused()` unconditionally returns `true` — the leader halts all further replication to that peer until the snapshot completes:\\n\\n```go\\ncase StateSnapshot:\\n    return true  // always paused\\n```\\n\\n#### Step 5 — Follower acknowledges and resumes replication\\n\\nOn the follower side, [`handleSnapshot()` in `raft/raft.go`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/raft.go?L1393-1404) applies the snapshot via `restore()`, then sends a `MsgAppResp` back to the leader. The leader uses this to transition the follower back to `StateProbe` → `StateReplicate` and resume normal log replication.\\n\\n---\\n\\n### Summary\\n\\n| Component | File | Role https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/deepsearch/1f1334ff-561c-48b0-b699-728b79474a39\ncreated: 2026-03-01T20:03:53Z\nupdated: 2026-03-01T20:06:44Z\n---\n\n# Find where ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable is defined and how the snapshot availability is checked when a node attempts to rejoin a Raft cluster for log catch-up in etcd-io/etcd\n\nNow I have a complete picture. Here's a comprehensive breakdown:\n\n---\n\n## `ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable` — Definition and Usage\n\n### 1. Definition\n\n`ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable` is defined in [`raft/storage.go` (line 38)](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/storage.go?L36-38):\n\n```go\n// ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable is returned by the Storage interface when the required\n// snapshot is temporarily unavailable.\nvar ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable = errors.New(\"snapshot is temporarily unavailable\")\n```\n\nIt is specified as part of the `Storage` interface contract on the [`Snapshot()` method (lines 67–71)](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/storage.go?L67-71):\n\n```go\n// Snapshot returns the most recent snapshot.\n// If snapshot is temporarily unavailable, it should return ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable,\n// so raft state machine could know that Storage needs some time to prepare\n// snapshot and call Snapshot later.\nSnapshot() (pb.Snapshot, error)\n```\n\nThis is a **signal contract**: custom `Storage` implementations (e.g., those with async or disk-backed snapshot generation) return this to tell the Raft state machine \"not yet, try again later.\" The built-in [`MemoryStorage.Snapshot()`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/storage.go?L165-170) never returns this error — it's always immediately available.\n\n---\n\n### 2. How Snapshot Availability Is Checked During Log Catch-Up\n\nWhen a **lagging node rejoins** the cluster and needs to catch up, the leader handles it via [`maybeSendAppend()` in `raft/raft.go` (lines 447–506)](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/raft.go?L447-506). Here's the full flow:\n\n#### Step 1 — Try to send log entries\nThe leader looks up the follower's [`Progress`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/tracker/progress.go?L30-80) tracker and tries to retrieve the entries from its next expected index (`pr.Next`):\n\n```go\nterm, errt := r.raftLog.term(pr.Next - 1)\nents, erre := r.raftLog.entries(pr.Next, r.maxMsgSize)\n```\n\n#### Step 2 — Fall back to snapshot if entries are unavailable\nIf `errt != nil || erre != nil` (i.e., the required entries have been compacted away — the node is too far behind), the leader falls back to sending a full snapshot:\n\n```go\nif errt != nil || erre != nil { // send snapshot if we failed to get term or entries\n    if !pr.RecentActive {\n        // Ignore — follower hasn't been heard from recently\n        return false\n    }\n\n    m.Type = pb.MsgSnap\n    snapshot, err := r.raftLog.snapshot()  // calls l.storage.Snapshot()\n```\n\n#### Step 3 — Snapshot availability check\n\n[`raftLog.snapshot()`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/log.go?L170-175) first checks for an in-memory unstable snapshot, then delegates to the application's `Storage`:\n\n```go\nfunc (l *raftLog) snapshot() (pb.Snapshot, error) {\n    if l.unstable.snapshot != nil {\n        return *l.unstable.snapshot, nil\n    }\n    return l.storage.Snapshot()\n}\n```\n\nBack in `maybeSendAppend()`, **this is where `ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable` is caught** [(lines 469–474)](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/raft.go?L469-474):\n\n```go\nif err != nil {\n    if err == ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable {\n        r.logger.Debugf(\"%x failed to send snapshot to %x because snapshot is temporarily unavailable\", r.id, to)\n        return false  // ← silently bail; will retry on next tick\n    }\n    panic(err) // any other error is fatal\n}\n```\n\n- **If `ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable`**: returns `false` — no message is sent this tick. The Raft heartbeat/tick cycle will cause `maybeSendAppend()` to be called again on the next tick, retrying the snapshot.\n- **Any other error**: panics immediately (unrecoverable).\n\n#### Step 4 — Snapshot is sent and follower transitions to `StateSnapshot`\n\nIf the snapshot is available, the leader sends a `MsgSnap` message and transitions the follower's progress via [`pr.BecomeSnapshot(sindex)` (line 483)](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/raft.go?L483):\n\n```go\nm.Snapshot = snapshot\npr.BecomeSnapshot(sindex)  // sets pr.State = StateSnapshot, pr.PendingSnapshot = sindex\n```\n\nWhile in [`StateSnapshot`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/tracker/state.go?L32-33), `IsPaused()` unconditionally returns `true` — the leader halts all further replication to that peer until the snapshot completes:\n\n```go\ncase StateSnapshot:\n    return true  // always paused\n```\n\n#### Step 5 — Follower acknowledges and resumes replication\n\nOn the follower side, [`handleSnapshot()` in `raft/raft.go`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/sourcegraph.com/github.com/sourcegraph-testing/etcd/-/blob/raft/raft.go?L1393-1404) applies the snapshot via `restore()`, then sends a `MsgAppResp` back to the leader. The leader uses this to transition the follower back to `StateProbe` → `StateReplicate` and resume normal log replication.\n\n---\n\n### Summary\n\n| Component | File | Role |\n|---|---|---|\n| Error
